<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【须菩提。于意云何。佛可以具足色身见不。不也世尊。如来不应以具足色身见。何以故。如来说具足色身。即非具足色身。是名具足色身。须菩提。于意云何。如来可以具足诸相见不。不也世尊。如来不应以具足诸相见。何以故。如来说诸相具足即非具足。是名诸相具足。】<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">如来色身具足圆满，具三十二相，相具八十随形好。这不过是对众生根机，方便说而已。其实十方如来，相好光明不可思议。十方诸佛，色具无量相，相具无量好也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">若以色相取佛，不见佛之法身。所以当世尊问须菩提，佛可以具足色身见不？须菩提回答说，不也世尊！如来说具足色身，即非具足色身，是名具足色身。如来说诸相具足，即非具足，是名诸相具足。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="margin-right:.1gd">此是说明相如幻，是假非真，不应以假相取佛。若人取著假相，便非发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提心。</p>
<p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="margin-right:.1gd"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a21"></a><span style="color:#333399">非说所说分第二十一<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【须菩提。汝勿谓如来作是念。我当有所说法。莫作是念。何以故。若人言如来有所说法即为谤佛。不能解我所说故。须菩提。说法者无法可说。是名说法。尔时慧命须菩提白佛言。世尊。颇有众生于未来世。闻说是法生信心不。佛言。须菩提。彼非众生非不众生。何以故。须菩提。众生众生者。如来说非众生。是名众生。】<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！汝勿谓如来作是念，我当有所说法……</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">法离名相，故不可取不可说。法不可得，故不可取不可说。法性空，故不可取不可说。所以若谓如来有所说法，即为谤佛，不解佛所说义。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！说法者无法可说，是名说法。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">说法者无法可说，因为诸法性空，诸法无相，所以无法可说。是名说法，说法者，唯是宣说假名也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">尔时慧命须菩提白佛言，世尊！颇有众生，于未来世，闻说是法，生信心不？</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">慧命是对比丘的尊称，有时亦称为慧寿，或具寿。是称叹比丘法身慧命之词也。法身以智慧为寿命，故称慧命。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提疑问说，能有众生，于未来世，闻说是法生信心吗？</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">如来回答说，须菩提！彼非众生，非不众生。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">所谓众生，是众缘和合而生者。换句话说，既闻‘众生’，即知此法无有自性。以无自性，则无此法。既无此法，故曰彼非众生。法无自性，故能随缘幻现假有。以假有故，故曰非不众生。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">诸法缘起，以缘起故，乃现诸法。法以缘现，定无自性。以无自性故，名曰性空。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">空不自空，以无自性故空，是知空者，即无自性也。而无自性者，即缘起也。所以缘起无自性，即是性空。性空无自性，即是缘起。简单来说，缘起即是性空，性空即是缘起。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">以缘起即是性空故，所以说彼非众生。以性空即是缘起故，所以说非不众生。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">何以故？须菩提！众生众生者，如来说非众生，是名众生。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">文中两个众生重叠，前边众生二字，是呼众生之名。后边众生二字，是欲作解释之词。所以这句话，应该这样写，‘众生，众生者。’</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">如来解释众生的意义说，如来说非众生，以缘起性空故。是名众生，以性空缘起故。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a22"></a><span style="color:#333399">无法可得分第二十二<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【须菩提白佛言。世尊。佛得阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。为无所得耶。如是如是。须菩提。我于阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。乃至无有少法可得是名阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。】<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提白佛言，世尊！佛得阿耨多罗三藐三菩提，为无所得耶？</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">佛法宗缘起，而缘起法性空无所得。缘起无自性，故无所得。性空无自性，亦复无所得。即此无所得，即名毕竟空，毕竟空是阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。故阿耨多罗三藐三菩提，即名无所得。不得一切法，即得阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。不见一切法，即见阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。故佛得阿耨多罗三藐三菩提，为无所得也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">佛印可曰，如是如是，我于阿耨多罗三藐三菩提，乃至无有少法可得，是名阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">阿耨多罗三藐三菩提即毕竟空故，所以乃至无有少法可得，只是假名阿耨多罗三藐三菩提而已。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a23"></a><span style="color:#333399">净心行善分第二十三<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【复次须菩提。是法平等无有高下。是名阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。以无我无人无众生无寿者。修一切善法则得阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。须菩提。所言善法者。如来说非善法是名善法。】<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">复次须菩提！是法平等，无有高下，是名阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">是法者，即阿耨多罗三藐三菩提也。阿耨多罗三藐三菩提毕竟空故，所以平等无有高下。离诸相故，所以平等无有高下。平等无有高下，则无分别，无分别则不可得。所谓阿耨多罗三藐三菩提者，只是假名而已。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">以无我无人无众生无寿者，修一切善法，则得阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">此言若人不取于相，则证无上菩提。故言无我人众寿相修一切善法，则得无上菩提。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">因为无我相无人相无众生相无寿者相，则于心不起贪嗔痴。心无贪嗔痴，自然身无杀盗淫，口无恶口妄语绮语两舌，故能修一切善法。此十善业又名十种净戒，是无上菩提根本。三业清净，足以成佛。故曰则得阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！所言善法者，如来说非善法，是名善法。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">所言善法者，亦复取相之言也。故曰即非善法，是名善法。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a24"></a><span style="color:#333399">福智无比分第二十四<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【须菩提。若三千大千世界中所有诸须弥山王。如是等七宝聚有人持用布施。若人以此般若波罗蜜经乃至四句偈等。受持读诵为他人说。于前福德百分不及一。百千万亿分乃至算数譬喻所不能及。】<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">这一分仍是说有相福德，不及无相福德为胜。因为有相之法，徒有其名，而无实义故。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">文显易明，不劳赘解。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a25"></a><span style="color:#333399">化无所化分第二十五<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【须菩提。于意云何。汝等勿谓如来作是念。我当度众生。须菩提。莫作是念。何以故。实无有众生如来度者。若有众生如来度者。如来则有我人众生寿者。须菩提。如来说有我者则非有我。而凡夫之人以为有我。须菩提。凡夫者如来说则非凡夫。】<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！于意云何？汝勿谓如来作是念，我当度众生。须菩提！莫作是念，何以故？实无有众生如来度者，若有众生如来度者，如来则有我人众生寿者。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">所谓众生，是众因缘所生法。因缘所生法，皆悉是空，六道众生一皆如是，故实无有众生如来度者。若谓有众生如来度者，那么如来便是取著于相。故曰如来则有我人众生寿者。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！如来说有我者，则非有我。而凡夫之人，以为有我。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">这句话的意思便是说，如来说有我者，则非有我，是名有我。如来所说有我者，只是假名，而非真实法性，以真实法性不可说故。而所说者，尽是假名。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">凡夫之人贪著假名相，故以为有我也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！凡夫者，如来说则非凡夫。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">凡夫者，亦是假名，故凡夫者，则非凡夫，是名凡夫耳。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">这一分的意旨，仍是说明，发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提心者，应降伏其取相心也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a26"></a><span style="color:#333399">法身非相分第二十六<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【须菩提。于意云何。可以三十二相观如来不。须菩提言。如是如是。以三十二相观如来。佛言。须菩提。若以三十二相观如来者。转轮圣王则是如来。须菩提白佛言。世尊。如我解佛所说义。不应以三十二相观如来。尔时世尊而说偈言<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal">&nbsp;</span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">若以色见我<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>以音声求我</span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">是人行邪道<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>不能见如来】</span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！于意云何？可以三十二相观如来不？</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">前文第十三分，谓可以三十二相见如来不？今文则云可以三十二相观如来不？前文用见字，后文用观字，于是有人言，观字与见字意义不同。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">其实恐怕无如此分别。我们虽不知原文如何，但菩提流支译本，前文后文均用‘见’字。义净三藏译本，前文后文均用‘观’字。可能只有罗什大师，有如是分别罢？！</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提言，如是如是，以三十二相观如来。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">因为佛之报身，具三十二相，为三大阿僧祇劫所修得者。故须菩提言，如是如是，以三十二相观如来。我们要知道，若以三十二相观如来，便是取相之见。所以如来马上纠正说：</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！若以三十二相观如来者，转轮圣王则是如来。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">因为转轮圣王福报很大，亦具三十二相。不过较佛，具体而微罢了。佛言须菩提！你若以三十二相观如来，只取其相的话，那么转轮圣王便是如来了。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">于是须菩提马上改口说，如我解佛所说义，不应以三十二相观如来。因为离一切诸相，即名如来也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">尔时世尊而说偈言：若以色见我，以音声求我，是人行邪道，不能见如来。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">若以色声香味触法六尘见我，此人便是行于邪道，不能见如来也。因为六尘有生有灭，而如来无生无灭。六尘是无常法，如来非无常法。六尘是败坏法，如来非败坏法。六尘是虚妄之相，如来是诸法实性。所以若以相取如来者，是人行邪道不能见如来也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">是故发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提心者，应降伏其取相心也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a27"></a><span style="color:#333399">无断无灭分第二十七<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【须菩提。汝若作是念。如来不以具足相故。得阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。须菩提。莫作是念。如来不以具足相故。得阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。须菩提。若作是念。发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提者说诸法断灭相。莫作是念。何以故。发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提心者。于法不说断灭相。】<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！汝若作是念，如来不以具足相故，得阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。须菩提！莫作是念，如来不以具足相故，得阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">这段经文，我们可以从两方面去了解。第一，阿耨多罗三藐三菩提，是不可得法。不可以具足相得，亦不可不以具足相得。所谓具足相者，乃具足三十二相也。第二，非是相外另有无相，亦非于无相外另有诸相。而是相即无相，无相即相。相不异无相，无相不异相。见相即是见无相，知无相即是知诸相。因为诸相缘起，即是无相。若知相即无相，当知无相即相矣。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">如果有人相外取于无相，此人便是著于无相之相。故曰不可以作是念‘如来不以具足相故，得阿耨多罗三藐三菩提。’</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！若作是念，发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提者，说诸法断灭相。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">何谓断灭？有外立空，此空即是断灭。如果空外立有，此有便是常。当知有不异空，空不异有。有即是空，空即是有。有为空之有，故空彻于有。以空彻有故，虽有而非常。空为有之空，故有彻于空。以有彻空故，虽空而非断。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">故于第一义中，有全是空，无有而非空。空全是有，无空而非有。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">故佛告须菩提言，莫作是念！何以故？发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提心者，于法不说断灭相。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">发无上菩提心者，契乎中道，故于法不说断灭相。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a28"></a><span style="color:#333399">不受不贪分第二十八<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【须菩提。若菩萨以满恒河沙等世界七宝布施。若复有人知一切法无我得成于忍。此菩萨胜前菩萨所得功德。须菩提。以诸菩萨不受福德故。须菩提白佛言。世尊。云何菩萨不受福德。须菩提。菩萨所作福德不应贪著。是故说不受福德。】<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！若菩萨以满恒河沙等世界七宝布施，若复有人知一切法无我得成于忍，此菩萨胜前菩萨所得功德。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">满恒河沙等世界七宝布施，乃是有相功德，假而非实。知一切法无我得成于忍，是真实功德，其功德无量。故前者功德，不能与后者相较。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">依探玄记，我有四种。一、真我，真如法性。二、自在我，以智慧为性。三、假我，五阴假合，唯识所现，似有主宰。四、执我，即分别与俱生二种我执，以所执为性。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">前二种我不无，后二种我非有也。所谓一切法无我者，遣后二种我也。若连前二种我并遣，法则断灭。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">以何义故，一切法无我？以法性空故，法相离故，法不可得故，法无分别故，一法界故，横遍竖穷故，心无所住故，法如如故。所以若复有人，知一切法无我得成于忍，其功德胜前功德。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">忍者，安忍也，忍可也，成清净信也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！以诸菩萨不受福德故。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">我为能受，福德为所受。若菩萨知一切法无我得成于忍者，则既无能受之我，亦无所受之法，故曰菩萨不受福德。以不受福德，成其无我义也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提白佛言，世尊！云何菩萨不受福德？须菩提！菩萨所作福德，不应贪著，是故说不受福德。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">所谓不应贪著者，即是心无所住也，不取于相也。若菩萨心有所住必生贪著，取著于相必生贪著。若生贪著，便不能发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提心。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提心者，若知一切法无我得成于忍，则能心无贪著。无有贪著，则能心无所住，不取于相，乃能成就无上功德。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a29"></a><span style="color:#333399">威仪寂静分第二十九<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【须菩提。若有人言如来若来若去若坐若卧。是人不解我所说义。何以故。如来者无所从来亦无所去故名如来。】<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！若有人言，如来若来若去若坐若卧，是人不解我所说义。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">来去坐卧是佛威仪，故昭明太子判此分为威仪寂静分。其实此分仍是在明法性离相也。大家千万莫听说无来无去无坐无卧，便作决定无来去坐卧会。如果那样，便又落断灭了。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">大家当会于相离相义。来而无来，去而无去，坐而无坐，卧而无卧。何以故？因为法性空寂，其相皆假。故来实无来相，以来相因缘幻有，假而非实故。去实无去相，以其相假故。坐实无坐相，以其相假故。卧实无卧相，以其相假故。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">若人以相取佛，则不悟如来法身，不见实相，故曰是人不解我所说义。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">何以故？如来者，无所从来，亦无所去，故名如来。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">如来者，表法性身。法性空故，是以无来无去。法性无相故，是以无来无去。法性不可得故，是以无来无去。若会空、无相、不可得义，便知此‘无来无去’亦无也。此之谓毕竟空。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">大家千万莫执相而求，认为有个如来，而这个如来，是无来无去的。当知那还是以相取佛，不解如来真实义也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a30"></a><span style="color:#333399">一合理相分第三十<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【须菩提。若善男子善女人。以三千大千世界碎为微尘。于意云何。是微尘众宁为多不。甚多世尊。何以故。若是微尘众实有者。佛则不说是微尘众。所以者何。佛说微尘众则非微尘众。是名微尘众。世尊。如来所说三千大千世界则非世界。是名世界。何以故。若世界实有者则是一合相。如来说一合相则非一合相。是名一合相。须菩提。一合相者则是不可说。但凡夫之人贪著其事。】<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">这一分是直显实相理体。实相理体者，性相圆融，二谛融通。性是无碍之理，相是无尽之事。以理融事，以事契理，是谓实相理体。一合相者，即实相理体也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！若善男子善女人，以三千大千世界碎为微尘，于意云何？是微尘众宁为多不？甚多世尊！何以故？若是微尘众实有者，佛则不说是微尘众，是名微尘众。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">微尘众多者，是其相也。微尘众实有者，则是究竟性也。法若究竟，则非一切法。故曰若微尘众实有者，佛则不说是微尘众。因为佛说微尘众者，只是假名也。所以佛说微尘众者，则非实有微尘众，而是假名微尘众也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">世尊！如来所说三千大千世界，则非世界，是名世界。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">其中道理，寻上文同理可知。因为世界是微尘所成，微尘既是假相，故世界亦是假相也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">何以故？若世界实有者，则是一合相。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">换句话说，若世界究竟，则是实相也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">一切法皆悉性空，其理无二，故曰‘一’。性空则能随缘而起万法，万法同一性空，融通无碍，故曰合。此则一合相也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">古德谈一合相，多从理上解释。例如六祖谓：心有所得，即非一合相。心无所得，即是一合相。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">此是从理上说。心有所得者，乃心有所住也，取著于相也。心有所住，取著于相，则如人入闇，不见实相。故心有所得，即是分别，即是执著，故非一合相。心无所得，则融通无碍，故为一合相。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">佛国勤禅师亦说：但向十二时中，上不见有诸佛，下不见有众生，外不见有山河大地，内不见有见闻觉知，好恶长短打成一片。一一拈出，更无异见。此则一合相理，历然明矣。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">此亦是从理上说。言修行人，不取相，莫分别，便是一合相理。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">我们现在从事上说明一合相理，以配合古德之说。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">例如微尘是一，而此一微尘即十方分合成。十方者，即上下东南西北及四维。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">微尘者，非微尘也。何以故？以微尘即十方分合成，于十方分外，更无微尘可得。呼为微尘者，徒有其名而无实义也。故微尘者，不过十方分和合之假相。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">微尘本空，由十方分和合而现假有其相，这便是一合相。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">同理可知，三千大千世界亦是十方分和合而成。世界本空，因缘和合假有其相，故名一合相。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">我们再举粗浅的例子说明。例如地球，实际上是山河大地人物等所合成。离开山河大地人物以外，实在没有个地球可得也。故地球即是一合相。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">既然法性空，故不应有住生心。既然和合相假，故不应取著于相。心无所住，不取于相，如是方为善男子善女人，发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提心也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">如来说一合相，则非一合相，是名一合相。须菩提！一合相者，则是不可说，但凡夫之人贪著其事。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">一合相是实相，实相无相，故不可说。但凡夫之人取相，故贪著其事，以为实有一合相也。菩萨不尔，以菩萨不取于相，不贪著其事故，所以不受其假相之福德也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">所以善男子善女人，发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提心，心无所住便是一合相理。不取于相，便是一合相理。无我相人相众生相寿者相，便是一合相理。心无贪著，便是一合相理。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a31"></a><span style="color:#333399">知见不生分第三十一<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【须菩提。若人言佛说我见人见众生见寿者见。须菩提。于意云何。是人解我所说义不。世尊。是人不解如来所说义。何以故。世尊说我见人见众生见寿者见即非我见人见众生见寿者见。是名我见人见众生见寿者见。须菩提。发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提心者。于一切法。应如是知如是见如是信解不生法相。须菩提。所言法相者。如来说即非法相。是名法相。】<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！若人言佛说我见人见众生见寿者见。须菩提！于意云何？是人解我所说义不？世尊！是人不解如来所说义。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">金刚经旨在离相明性，若谓佛说我人众寿见，便是谓佛取相。若谓佛取相，便是谓佛未见性。若未见性，焉得名佛？故须菩提回答说，是人不解如来所说义。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">何以故？世尊说我见人见众生见寿者见，即非我见人见众生见寿者见，是名我见人见众生见寿者见。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">佛于无名相法，而以名相说。故虽方便说我见人见众生见寿者见，即非我见人见众生见寿者见，只是方便假名而已。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提心者，于一切法，应如是知，如是见，如是信解，不生法相。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">发无上菩提心者，应知一切相假，应知一切性空。以一切相假，故一切性空。以一切性空，故一切相假。相假不异性空，性空不异相假。相假即是性空，性空即是相假。发阿耨多罗三藐三菩提心者，于一切法，应如是知，如是见，如是信解，莫生法相也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！所言法相者，如来说即非法相，是名法相。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">文义准上自明，不另。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a32"></a><span style="color:#333399">应化非真分第三十二<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">【须菩提。若有人以满无量阿僧祇世界七宝持用布施。若有善男子善女人发菩萨心者。持于此经乃至四句偈等。受持读诵为人演说其福胜彼。云何为人演说。不取于相如如不动。何以故<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">一切有为法<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>如梦幻泡影</span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">如露亦如电<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>应作如是观</span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal">&nbsp;</span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal"><span style="color:teal">佛说是经已。长老须菩提及诸比丘比丘尼优婆塞优婆夷。一切世间天人阿修罗。闻佛所说皆大欢喜。信受奉行。】<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">须菩提！若有人以满无量阿僧祇世界七宝持用布施，若有善男子善女人发菩萨心者（应为发菩提心者），持于此经，乃至四句偈等，受持读诵为人演说，其福胜彼。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">最后再度叮咛，假相福德，不及无相福德为胜。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">云何为人演说，不取于相，如如不动。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">不取于相，以相假故。如如不动，以性空故。若人如是知，如是见，如是信解，知见信解诸法相假性空，则能为人演说矣。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">何以故？一切有为法，如梦幻泡影，如露亦如电，应作如是观。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">何谓有为法？有为法者，有生、住、灭三相也。简言之，生灭法即有为法也。故有为法生灭无常，如梦幻泡影，如露如电也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">云何是无生灭法，相假故无生灭，性空故无生灭，不可得法无有生灭，无有定法故无生灭。所以偈中之意，谓菩萨应如是观一切相假也。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">佛说是经已，长老须菩提，及诸比丘比丘尼优婆塞优婆夷，一切世间天人阿修罗，闻佛所说，皆大欢喜，信受奉行。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">于是这部金刚经，佛演说圆满。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="margin-right:.1gd">这部金刚经，我们总算讲完了。最后我有几句话，要告诉各位。金刚经旨在显示法性。其实不只金刚经，七百二十多卷般若经，皆在显示法性。所以我们读金刚经，不可只解名相，而不求了悟法性。如果只知执相而求，可谓与金刚经咫尺天涯了。希望大家切记切记！（弟子慧修敬记）</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">金刚般若波罗蜜经讲记终</p>
<p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="margin-right:.1gd"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="margin-right:.1gd;text-indent:0cm;mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-char-indent-size:0cm"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
